@IDENTITY psdiesel  = p_iea_diesel08  / eff_veh08_x

@IDENTITY psgasoline  = p_iea_gasoline06  / eff_veh06_x

@IDENTITY psheat  = pheat  / eff_heat_x

@IDENTITY psel  = pel  / eff_el_x

:EQSERV17_08
@ADD SERVTJ17_08  SERVTJ17_08_A

:EQSERV17_06
@ADD SERVTJ17_06  SERVTJ17_06_A

'scen_behav_pkw  Verhaltensänderung im Szenario(0% bedeutet keine veraenderung zum Baseline)

pkw_verhaltensfaktor  = scen_behav_pkw

servtj17_06_corr  = servtj17_06  * (1  + pkw_verhaltensfaktor)

servtj17_08_corr  = servtj17_08  * (1  + pkw_verhaltensfaktor)

@IDENTITY tj17_06  = servtj17_06_corr  / eff_veh06_x
@IDENTITY tj17_08  = servtj17_08_corr  / eff_veh08_x

@IDENTITY tj17_06_i  = s_pkw_i  * tj17_06
@IDENTITY tj17_06_ii  = s_pkw_ii  * tj17_06
@IDENTITY tj17_06_iii  = s_pkw_iii  * tj17_06
@IDENTITY tj17_06_iv  = s_pkw_iv  * tj17_06
@IDENTITY tj17_06_v  = s_pkw_v  * tj17_06

@IDENTITY tj17_08_i  = s_pkw_i  * tj17_08
@IDENTITY tj17_08_ii  = s_pkw_ii  * tj17_08
@IDENTITY tj17_08_iii  = s_pkw_iii  * tj17_08
@IDENTITY tj17_08_iv  = s_pkw_iv  * tj17_08
@IDENTITY tj17_08_v  = s_pkw_v  * tj17_08

'############# VEHICLES ELECTRO ################
'Die ServiceNF per Pkw von Elektro-Pkw is so berechnet, sodass die Fahrleistung von Pkw-Benzin = Pkw-Elektro
'0.15.. und 0.809... sind kwh/km von Elektro und Benzin in 2000 (=indexjahr 1) - noetig fuer service umrechnung
' der teil mit TREND geht vno 0 in 2000 auf 1 in 2050 - fahrleistung von Eletkro nähert sich also langsam
'0.75 steht dafür dass Elektropkw eher für kurzstrecken verwendet werden und ca 75% des benzinpkw fahren

@IDENTITY servtj17_22_per_pkw  = ((servtj17_06  / pkw06)  * (0.1511976  / 0.80984749)  * (@TREND  - 5)  / 50 )  * 0.75

@IDENTITY servtj17_22pkw  = servtj17_22_per_pkw  * pkw22  * (1  + pkw_verhaltensfaktor)

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw  = servtj17_22pkw  / eff_veh22_x

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw_i  = s_pkw_i  * tj17_22pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw_ii  = s_pkw_ii  * tj17_22pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw_iii  = s_pkw_iii  * tj17_22pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw_iv  = s_pkw_iv  * tj17_22pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_22pkw_v  = s_pkw_v  * tj17_22pkw

'############# VEHICLES NAT GAS ################
'service tj pro pkw wie diesel + 15%

@IDENTITY servtj17_14pkw  = ((1.15)  * servtj17_08  / pkw08)  * pkw14  * (1  + pkw_verhaltensfaktor)

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw  = servtj17_14pkw  / eff_veh08_x

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw_i  = s_pkw_i  * tj17_14pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw_ii  = s_pkw_ii  * tj17_14pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw_iii  = s_pkw_iii  * tj17_14pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw_iv  = s_pkw_iv  * tj17_14pkw

@IDENTITY tj17_14pkw_v  = s_pkw_v  * tj17_14pkw

'#############APPLICATION - HEAT################

@IDENTITY k_app_real  = k_app_total  / pcp_app_pp

@IDENTITY k_app_real_i  = k_app_i  / pcp_app_pp

@IDENTITY k_app_real_ii  = k_app_ii  / pcp_app_pp

@IDENTITY k_app_real_iii  = k_app_iii  / pcp_app_pp

@IDENTITY k_app_real_iv  = k_app_iv  / pcp_app_pp

:EQSERV17_HEAT
@ADD SERVTJ17_HEAT  SERVTJ17_HEAT_A

'scen_behav_heat Verhaltensänderung im Szenario(0% bedeutet keine veraenderung zum Baseline)

heat_verhaltensfaktor  = scen_behav_heat

servtj17_heat_corr  = servtj17_heat  * (1  + heat_verhaltensfaktor)

@IDENTITY tj17_heat  = servtj17_heat_corr  / eff_heat_x

'###disaggregation into householddemand###

@IDENTITY tj17_heat_i  = (k_app_real_i  / k_app_real)  * (tj17_heat)

@IDENTITY tj17_heat_ii  = (k_app_real_ii  / k_app_real)  * (tj17_heat)

@IDENTITY tj17_heat_iii  = (k_app_real_iii  / k_app_real)  * (tj17_heat)

@IDENTITY tj17_heat_iv  = (k_app_real_iv  / k_app_real)  * (tj17_heat)

@IDENTITY tj17_heat_v  = (k_app_real_v  / k_app_real)  * (tj17_heat)

@IDENTITY tj17_22vid  = servtj17_22_corr  / eff_el_x

'++FUEL++

'###COAL PRODUCTS 01 02 03 04 05 #####

@IDENTITY CP_bp10_i  = ( (tj17_01_i  + tj17_02_i  + tj17_03_i  + tj17_04_i  + tj17_05_i)  / zrcp10 )  * pcp10_tjx

@IDENTITY CP_bp10_ii  = ( (tj17_01_ii  + tj17_02_ii  + tj17_03_ii  + tj17_04_ii  + tj17_05_ii)  / zrcp10 )  * pcp10_tjx

@ADD K_APP_III  K_APP_III_A

@ADD K_APP_IV  K_APP_IV_A

k_app_v  = ((c_v_app  + (log_g_app  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_app  * log_G_app  * ((yd_v  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_v  / log_normyd_hh_app))  * (log_G_app  / log_f0_app  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_app  * households_v)  * pcp_app_pp
@ADD K_APP_V  K_APP_V_A

@IDENTITY k_app_total  = k_app_i  + k_app_ii  + k_app_iii  + k_app_iv  + k_app_v

'##
'######################## K HOUSING  ######################
'#show
'*************************************
' houses all
'*************************************

@IDENTITY K_houstot_i  = K_ownhouses_i  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_i

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_i  = K_houstot_i  * p_houses

@IDENTITY K_houstot_ii  = K_ownhouses_ii  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_ii

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_ii  = K_houstot_ii  * p_houses

@IDENTITY K_houstot_iii  = K_ownhouses_iii  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_iii

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_iii  = K_houstot_iii  * p_houses

@IDENTITY K_houstot_iv  = K_ownhouses_iv  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_iv

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_iv  = K_houstot_iv  * p_houses

@IDENTITY K_houstot_v  = K_ownhouses_v  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_v

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_v  = K_houstot_v  * p_houses

@IDENTITY K_houstot_total  = K_ownhouses_total  / p_houses  + K_renthouses_total

@IDENTITY K_houstotN_total  = K_houstot_total  * p_houses

@IDENTITY interest_houses  = spread_houses  * interest_durable

'*************************************
'own houses
'*************************************

k_ownhouses_i  = ((c_i_hou  + (log_g_hou  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_hou  * log_G_hou  * ((yd_i  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_i  / log_normyd_hh_hou))  * (log_G_hou  / log_f0_hou  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_hou  * households_i)  * p_houses
@ADD K_OWNHOUSES_I  K_OWNHOUSES_I_A

k_ownhouses_ii  = ((c_ii_hou  + (log_g_hou  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_hou  * log_G_hou  * ((yd_ii  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_ii  / log_normyd_hh_hou))  * (log_G_hou  / log_f0_hou  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_hou  * households_ii)  * p_houses
@ADD K_OWNHOUSES_II  K_OWNHOUSES_II_A

k_ownhouses_iii  = ((c_iii_hou  + (log_g_hou  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_hou  * log_G_hou  * ((yd_iii  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_iii  / log_normyd_hh_hou))  * (log_G_hou  / log_f0_hou  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_hou  * households_iii)  * p_houses
@ADD K_OWNHOUSES_III  K_OWNHOUSES_III_A

k_ownhouses_iv  = ((c_iv_hou  + (log_g_hou  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_hou  * log_G_hou  * ((yd_iv  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_iv  / log_normyd_hh_hou))  * (log_G_hou  / log_f0_hou  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_hou  * households_iv)  * p_houses
@ADD K_OWNHOUSES_IV  K_OWNHOUSES_IV_A

k_ownhouses_v  = ((c_v_hou  + (log_g_hou  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_hou  * log_G_hou  * ((yd_v  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_v  / log_normyd_hh_hou))  * (log_G_hou  / log_f0_hou  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_hou  * households_v)  * p_houses
@ADD K_OWNHOUSES_V  K_OWNHOUSES_V_A

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_total  = k_ownhouses_i  + k_ownhouses_ii  + k_ownhouses_iii  + k_ownhouses_iv  + k_ownhouses_v

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_i  = k_ownhouses_i  / p_houses

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_ii  = k_ownhouses_ii  / p_houses

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_iii  = k_ownhouses_iii  / p_houses

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_iv  = k_ownhouses_iv  / p_houses

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_v  = k_ownhouses_v  / p_houses

@IDENTITY k_ownhouses_real_total  = k_ownhouses_real_i  + k_ownhouses_real_ii  + k_ownhouses_real_iii  + k_ownhouses_real_iv  + k_ownhouses_real_v

'Rent houses
'*************************************

@IDENTITY K_renthouses_i  = Rent_to_pop_i  * Pop_i

'######################## K VEHICLES  ######################

k_veh_i  = ((c_i_veh  + (log_g_veh  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_veh  * log_G_veh  * ((yd_i  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_i  / log_normyd_hh_veh))  * (log_G_veh  / log_f0_veh  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_veh  * households_i)  * pcp_veh_pp
@ADD K_VEH_I  K_VEH_I_A

k_veh_ii  = ((c_ii_veh  + (log_g_veh  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_veh  * log_G_veh  * ((yd_ii  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_ii  / log_normyd_hh_veh))  * (log_G_veh  / log_f0_veh  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_veh  * households_ii)  * pcp_veh_pp
@ADD K_VEH_II  K_VEH_II_A

k_veh_iii  = ((c_iii_veh  + (log_g_veh  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_veh  * log_G_veh  * ((yd_iii  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_iii  / log_normyd_hh_veh))  * (log_G_veh  / log_f0_veh  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_veh  * households_iii)  * pcp_veh_pp
@ADD K_VEH_III  K_VEH_III_A

k_veh_iv  = ((c_iv_veh  + (log_g_veh  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_veh  * log_G_veh  * ((yd_iv  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_iv  / log_normyd_hh_veh))  * (log_G_veh  / log_f0_veh  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_veh  * households_iv)  * pcp_veh_pp
@ADD K_VEH_IV  K_VEH_IV_A

k_veh_v  = ((c_v_veh  + (log_g_veh  * (1  / (1  + exp(-log_k_veh  * log_G_veh  * ((yd_v  / pcp_00_pp)  / households_v  / log_normyd_hh_veh))  * (log_G_veh  / log_f0_veh  - 1)))))  * log_norm_k_veh  * households_v)  * pcp_veh_pp
@ADD K_VEH_V  K_VEH_V_A

@IDENTITY k_veh_real_iv  = k_veh_iv  / pcp_veh_pp

@IDENTITY k_veh_real_v  = k_veh_v  / pcp_veh_pp

@IDENTITY veh_pop_i  = (1000000  * k_veh_real_i)  / (pkw_val2005_i  * pop_i)

@IDENTITY veh_pop  = (veh_pop_i  * pop_i  + veh_pop_ii  * pop_ii  + veh_pop_iii  * pop_iii  + veh_pop_iv  * pop_iv  + veh_pop_v  * pop_v)  / (pop)

@IDENTITY pkw_total  = veh_pop  * Pop

@ADD K_VID_IV  K_VID_IV_A

@IDENTITY deprate_ii  = (K_veh_ii  / K_Durables_ii)  * deprate_veh  + (K_vid_ii  / K_Durables_ii)  * deprate_vid  + (K_ownhouses_ii  / K_Durables_ii)  * deprate_hou  + (K_app_ii  / K_Durables_ii)  * deprate_app

@IDENTITY wages_I  = va_wages  * s_va_wage_I

@IDENTITY wages_IV  = va_wages  * s_va_wage_IV

'  total  Surplus wird in Part 7 berechnet  als  "va_surplus_net"  aus SUT dieser wird mit dem hist Anteil der Haushalte an den Gesamt_Surplus (aus NatAccount& SUT) multipliziert

@IDENTITY OpSurplusHH_I  = s_va_Surplus_I  * s_va_NetSurplus4hh  * va_surplus_net

@IDENTITY OpSurplusHH_II  = s_va_Surplus_II  * s_va_NetSurplus4hh  * va_surplus_net

@IDENTITY OpSurplusHH_IV  = s_va_Surplus_IV  * s_va_NetSurplus4hh  * va_surplus_net

@IDENTITY OpSurplusHH_v  = s_va_surplus_v  * s_va_NetSurplus4hh  * va_surplus_net

' profit hh ist exogen (lt kurt ) extrapoliert
'@IDENTITY ProfitHH_total  = ProfitHH_I  + ProfitHH_II  + ProfitHH_III  + ProfitHH_IV  + ProfitHH_v

@IDENTITY ProfitHH_I  = s_Profit_q_I  * ProfitHH_total

@IDENTITY ProfitHH_II  = s_Profit_q_II  * ProfitHH_total

@IDENTITY ProfitHH_III  = s_Profit_q_III  * ProfitHH_total

@IDENTITY ProfitHH_IV  = s_Profit_q_IV  * ProfitHH_total

@IDENTITY ProfitHH_v  = s_Profit_q_v  * ProfitHH_total

'  Steuern leiten sich aus den einkommen ab

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_total  = TaxesHH_I  + TaxesHH_II  + TaxesHH_III  + TaxesHH_IV  + TaxesHH_v

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_I  = r_Tax_I  * ( wages_I  + OpSurplusHH_I  + ProfitHH_I)

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_II  = r_Tax_II  * ( wages_II  + OpSurplusHH_II  + ProfitHH_II)

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_III  = r_Tax_III  * ( wages_III  + OpSurplusHH_III  + ProfitHH_III)

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_IV  = r_Tax_IV  * ( wages_IV  + OpSurplusHH_IV  + ProfitHH_IV)

@IDENTITY TaxesHH_v  = r_Tax_v  * ( wages_v  + OpSurplusHH_v  + ProfitHH_v)

@IDENTITY SocContHH_total  = SocContHH_I  + SocContHH_II  + SocContHH_III  + SocContHH_IV  + SocContHH_v

@IDENTITY SocContHH_I  = r_SocCont_I  * wages_I

@IDENTITY SocContHH_II  = r_SocCont_II  * wages_II

@IDENTITY SocContHH_III  = r_SocCont_III  * wages_III

@IDENTITY SocContHH_IV  = r_SocCont_IV  * wages_IV

@IDENTITY SocContHH_v  = r_SocCont_v  * wages_v

'  Transfers sind vorerst als Anteil der PRoduktion implementiert  (Annahme dQ -> dTaxes -> dTransfers = ählnich)

@IDENTITY TransfHH_total  = TransfHH_I  + TransfHH_II  + TransfHH_III  + TransfHH_IV  + TransfHH_v

@IDENTITY TransfHH_I  = r_Transfer_q_I  * q00

@IDENTITY TransfHH_II  = r_Transfer_q_II  * q00

@IDENTITY TransfHH_III  = r_Transfer_q_III  * q00

@IDENTITY TransfHH_IV  = r_Transfer_q_IV  * q00

@IDENTITY TransfHH_v  = r_Transfer_q_v  * q00

'  Other incomes sind vorerst als Anteil der PRoduktion implementiert

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_total  = OtherIncHH_I  + OtherIncHH_II  + OtherIncHH_III  + OtherIncHH_IV  + OtherIncHH_v

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_I  = r_Otherinc_q_I  * q00

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_II  = r_Otherinc_q_II  * q00

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_III  = r_Otherinc_q_III  * q00

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_IV  = r_Otherinc_q_IV  * q00

@IDENTITY OtherIncHH_v  = r_Otherinc_q_v  * q00

@IDENTITY YD_total  = YD_I  + YD_II  + YD_III  + YD_IV  + YD_v

@IDENTITY YD_I  = wages_I  + OpSurplusHH_I  + ProfitHH_I  - TaxesHH_I  - SocContHH_I  + TransfHH_I  + OtherIncHH_I

@IDENTITY YD_II  = wages_II  + OpSurplusHH_II  + ProfitHH_II  - TaxesHH_II  - SocContHH_II  + TransfHH_II  + OtherIncHH_II

@IDENTITY YD_III  = wages_III  + OpSurplusHH_III  + ProfitHH_III  - TaxesHH_III  - SocContHH_III  + TransfHH_III  + OtherIncHH_III

@IDENTITY YD_IV  = wages_IV  + OpSurplusHH_IV  + ProfitHH_IV  - TaxesHH_IV  - SocContHH_IV  + TransfHH_IV  + OtherIncHH_IV

@IDENTITY YD_v  = wages_v  + OpSurplusHH_v  + ProfitHH_v  - TaxesHH_v  - SocContHH_v  + TransfHH_v  + OtherIncHH_v

'##
'######################## CASH ON HAND ######################
'#show

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_i  = yd_i  + (1  - deprate_i)  * k_durables_i(-1)

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_ii  = yd_ii  + (1  - deprate_ii)  * k_durables_ii(-1)

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_iii  = yd_iii  + (1  - deprate_iii)  * k_durables_iii(-1)

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_iv  = yd_iv  + (1  - deprate_iv)  * k_durables_iv(-1)

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_v  = yd_v  + (1  - deprate_v)  * k_durables_v(-1)

@IDENTITY cash_on_hand_total  = cash_on_hand_i  + cash_on_hand_ii  + cash_on_hand_iii  + cash_on_hand_iv  + cash_on_hand_v
